We validated the following systems do not use the software affected by the Heartbleed Vulnerability:  SAM, FPDS-NG, FBO, eSRS, FSRS, CFDA, and WDOL. \nCPARS, PPIRS and FAPIIS have been updated to OpenSSL version 1.0.1g which resolved the vulnerability.
